    CaptionML=ENU=Estimate Lines per Part Open Budget;
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  CheckRelationSummaryEstimate;  //db, 08-05-11: C015230

                  IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN  //C015315
                    IF NOT IgnoreSummary THEN
                      InfoTxt := Text003
                    ELSE
                      InfoTxt := Text004;
                  END;

                  IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN  //C015315
                    IF NOT IgnoreSummary THEN
                      InfoTxt := Text006
                    ELSE
                      InfoTxt := Text007;
                  END;

                  IF IgnoreSummary THEN
                    InfoTxt2 := Text005;
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525002;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;

    { 1100525004;0;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012151;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               "Estimate Line".COPYFILTER("Estimate No.", "No.");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SummarySheetLine@1100525000 : Record 11012171;
                                  Customer@1100525001 : Record 18;
                                BEGIN
                                  TotalLabor := 0;
                                  TotalMaterial := 0;
                                  TotalSubcontracting := 0;
                                  TotalPlant := 0;
                                  TotalSundry := 0;
                                  TotalAssumption := 0;
                                  TotalEstimate := 0;

                                  DetermineSummarySheet(Estimate, SummarySheet);

                                  TempSummarySheetLine1.RESET;
                                  TempSummarySheetLine1.DELETEALL;
                                  TempSummarySheetLine2.RESET;
                                  TempSummarySheetLine2.DELETEALL;

                                  SummarySheetLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "No.");
                                  SummarySheetLine.SETRANGE(Summary, SummarySheet.Summary);
                                  SummarySheetLine.SETFILTER(Amount, '<>%1', 0);
                                  IF SummarySheetLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                    REPEAT
                                      TempSummarySheetLine1 := SummarySheetLine;
                                      TempSummarySheetLine1.INSERT;
                                      IF SummarySheetLine."Surcharge Over Row" <> Text000 THEN BEGIN
                                        TempSummarySheetLine2 := SummarySheetLine;
                                        TempSummarySheetLine2.INSERT;
                                      END;
                                    UNTIL SummarySheetLine.NEXT = 0;
                                  END;

                                  IF Customer.GET("Customer No.") THEN
                                    NameCustomer := Customer.Name;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525065;1;Column;No_Estimate        ;
               SourceExpr=Estimate."No." }

    { 1100525069;1;Column;Description_Estimate;

    { 1100525099;1;Column;NameCustomer_Estimate;

    { 1100528601;1;Column;ReportCurrencyCode_Estimate;

    { 1100525067;1;DataItem;Sub-Estimate     ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072074;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               "Estimate Line".COPYFILTER("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
                               "Estimate Line".COPYFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
                               "Estimate Line".COPYFILTER("Part Group", "Part Group");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  EstimateLine.RESET;
                                  EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
                                  EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
                                  IF NOT EstimateLine.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;  //C029756
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525047;2;DataItem;CommentLineSubEstimate;
               DataItemTable=Table11020595;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Table Name,Group,No.,Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Estimate Line No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Table Name=CONST(Estimate),
                                       Part Group=FILTER(''),
                                       Part=FILTER(''),
                                       Estimate Line No.=CONST(0));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT PrintText THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.) }

    { 1100525040;3;Column;LineNo_CommentLineSubEstimate;
               SourceExpr=CommentLineSubEstimate."Line No." }

    { 1100525038;3;Column;Comment_CommentLineSubEstimate;

    { 1100525061;2;DataItem;Estimate Part    ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072073;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               "Estimate Line".COPYFILTER("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
                               "Estimate Line".COPYFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
                               "Estimate Line".COPYFILTER("Part Group", "Part Group");
                               "Estimate Line".COPYFILTER(Part, Part);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  EstimateLine.RESET;
                                  EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
                                  EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
                                  EstimateLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", "Part Group");
                                  EstimateLine.SETRANGE(Part, Part);
                                  IF NOT EstimateLine.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;  //C029756

                                  IF TotalsPerChapter THEN
                                    Part2 := Chapter
                                  ELSE
                                    Part2 := Part;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group) }

    { 1100525072;3;Column;Part_EstimatePart  ;

    { 1100525079;3;DataItem;CommentLineEstimatePart;
               DataItemTable=Table11020595;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Table Name,Group,No.,Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Estimate Line No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Table Name=CONST(Estimate),
                                       Estimate Line No.=CONST(0));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT PrintText THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group),

    { 1100525051;4;Column;LineNo_CommentLineEstimatePart;
               SourceExpr=CommentLineEstimatePart."Line No." }

    { 1100525048;4;Column;Comment_CommentLineEstimatePart;
               SourceExpr=CommentLineEstimatePart.Comment }

    { 1100525006;3;DataItem;Estimate Line    ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072072;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Line No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  AssumptionLine@1100525000 : Boolean;
                                  SingleSubEstQuantity@1100528600 : Decimal;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost) AND
                                     (Quantity = 0) AND
                                     NOT PrintZeroLines
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales) AND
                                     ("Quantity (Sales)" = 0) AND
                                     NOT PrintZeroLines
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  AssumptionLine := FALSE;
                                  IF LineStatusFilter <> '' THEN
                                    AssumptionLine := EstLineInLineStatusFilter("Estimate Line");

                                  IF Recipe = '' THEN BEGIN
                                    CalculateTotalsWithOptions(FALSE);
                                    DetermineSurchEstLine("Estimate Line")
                                  END ELSE
                                    DetermineAmountRecipeEstLine("Estimate Line");

                                  IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
                                    EstimateLineQuantity := Quantity;
                                    EstimateLineHours := Hours;
                                    IF IsLCYReportCurrency THEN BEGIN
                                      EstimateLineLaborAmount := "Labor Cost Amount";
                                      EstimateLineMaterialAmount := "Material Cost Amount";
                                      EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := "Subcontracting Cost Amount";
                                      EstimateLinePlantAmount := "Plant Cost Amount";
                                      EstimateLineSundryAmount := "Sundry Cost Amount";
                                      EstimateLineAmount := "Cost Amount";
                                      EstimateLineCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total";
                                      EstimateLinePartTotal := EstimateLineAmount * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
                                      TotalLabor += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor";
                                      TotalMaterial += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material";
                                      TotalSubcontracting += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontracting";
                                      TotalPlant += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant";
                                      TotalSundry += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry";
                                      TotalEstimate +=
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontracting" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry";
                                    END ELSE IF IsFCYandSameReportCurrency("Currency Code") THEN BEGIN
                                      EstimateLineLaborAmount := "Labor Cost Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineMaterialAmount := "Material Cost Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := "Subcontr. Cost Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLinePlantAmount := "Plant Cost Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineSundryAmount := "Sundry Cost Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineAmount := "Cost Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLinePartTotal := EstimateLineAmount * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
                                      TotalLabor += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (FCY)";
                                      TotalMaterial += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material (FCY)";
                                      TotalSubcontracting += EstimateLineTotal."Cum. Subcontracting (FCY)";
                                      TotalPlant += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (FCY)";
                                      TotalSundry += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry (FCY)";
                                      TotalEstimate +=
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (FCY)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material (FCY)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cum. Subcontracting (FCY)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (FCY)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry (FCY)";
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      EstimateLineLaborAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Labor Cost Amount", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineMaterialAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Material Cost Amount", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Subcontracting Cost Amount", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLinePlantAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Plant Cost Amount", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineSundryAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Sundry Cost Amount", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Cost Amount", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineCumulativeTotal := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLinePartTotal := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineAmount * "Estimate Part".Quantity, FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalLabor += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalMaterial += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalSubcontracting += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontracting", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalPlant += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalSundry += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalEstimate +=
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE) +
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE) +
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontracting", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE) +
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE) +
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry", FALSE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                    END;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    EstimateLineQuantity := "Quantity (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLineHours := "Hours (Sales)";
                                    IF IsLCYReportCurrency THEN BEGIN
                                      EstimateLineLaborAmount := "Labor Sales Amount";
                                      EstimateLineMaterialAmount := "Material Sales Amount";
                                      EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := "Subcontracting Sales Amount";
                                      EstimateLinePlantAmount := "Plant Sales Amount";
                                      EstimateLineSundryAmount := "Sundry Sales Amount";
                                      EstimateLineAmount := "Sales Amount";
                                      EstimateLineCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total (Sales)";
                                      EstimateLinePartTotal := EstimateLineAmount * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
                                      TotalLabor += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (Sales)";
                                      TotalMaterial += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material (Sales)";
                                      TotalSubcontracting += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontr. (Sales)";
                                      TotalPlant += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (Sales)";
                                      TotalSundry += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry (Sales)";
                                      TotalEstimate +=
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (Sales)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material (Sales)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontr. (Sales)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (Sales)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry (Sales)";
                                    END ELSE IF IsFCYandSameReportCurrency("Currency Code") THEN BEGIN
                                      EstimateLineLaborAmount := "Labor Sales Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineMaterialAmount := "Material Sales Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := "Subcontr. Sales Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLinePlantAmount := "Plant Sales Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineSundryAmount := "Sundry Sales Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineAmount := "Sales Amount (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLineCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total (Sales) (FCY)";
                                      EstimateLinePartTotal := EstimateLineAmount * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
                                      TotalLabor += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (Sales) (FCY)";
                                      TotalMaterial += EstimateLineTotal."Cum. Material (Sales) (FCY)";
                                      TotalSubcontracting += EstimateLineTotal."Cum. Subcontr. (Sales) (FCY)";
                                      TotalPlant += EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (Sales) (FCY)";
                                      TotalSundry += EstimateLineTotal."Cum. Sundry (Sales) (FCY)";
                                      TotalEstimate +=
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (Sales) (FCY)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cum. Material (Sales) (FCY)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cum. Subcontr. (Sales) (FCY)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (Sales) (FCY)" +
                                        EstimateLineTotal."Cum. Sundry (Sales) (FCY)";
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      EstimateLineLaborAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Labor Sales Amount", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineMaterialAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Material Sales Amount", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Subcontracting Sales Amount", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLinePlantAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Plant Sales Amount", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineSundryAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Sundry Sales Amount", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineAmount := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY("Sales Amount", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLineCumulativeTotal := ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      EstimateLinePartTotal := EstimateLineAmount * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
                                      TotalLabor += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalMaterial += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalSubcontracting += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontr. (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalPlant += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalSundry += ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                      TotalEstimate +=
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE) +
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE) +
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontr. (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE) +
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE) +
                                        ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry (Sales)", TRUE, FALSE, TRUE);
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  Assumption := 0;
                                  IF AssumptionLine THEN BEGIN
                                    EstimateLineLaborAmount := 0;
                                    EstimateLineMaterialAmount := 0;
                                    EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := 0;
                                    EstimateLinePlantAmount := 0;
                                    EstimateLineSundryAmount := 0;
                                    Assumption := EstimateLineAmount;
                                    TotalAssumption += EstimateLineAmount * "Part Quantity";
                                  END;

                                  IF "Sub-Estimate"."Cumulative Frequency" <> 0 THEN
                                    SingleSubEstQuantity := "Part Quantity" / "Sub-Estimate"."Cumulative Frequency"
                                  ELSE
                                    SingleSubEstQuantity := 0;

                                  CumEstimateLineHours := EstimateLineHours * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineLaborAmount := EstimateLineLaborAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineMaterialAmount := EstimateLineMaterialAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLinePlantAmount := EstimateLinePlantAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineSundryAmount := EstimateLineSundryAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineAmount := EstimateLineAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;

                                  IF NOT PrintText THEN BEGIN  //db, 07-11-14: C018681
                                    "External Text" := '';
                                    "Internal Text" := '';
                                  END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part;
               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group),
                            Part=FIELD(Part) }

    { 1100525011;4;Column;EstimateNo_EstimateLine;
               IncludeCaption=Yes;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line"."Estimate No." }

    { 1100525012;4;Column;EstimateDescription_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line"."Estimate Description" }

    { 1100525013;4;Column;SubEstimateNo_EstimateLine;

    { 1100525015;4;Column;Part_EstimateLine  ;
               IncludeCaption=Yes;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line".Part }

    { 1100525039;4;Column;PartDescription_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line"."Part Description" }

    { 1100525046;4;Column;LineNo_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line"."Line No." }

    { 1100525043;4;Column;Description_EstimateLine;
               IncludeCaption=Yes;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line".Description }

    { 1100525017;4;Column;UnitofMeasure_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line"."Unit of Measure" }

    { 1100409001;4;Column;ExternalText_Text  ;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line"."External Text" }

    { 1100409000;4;Column;InternalText_Text  ;
               SourceExpr="Estimate Line"."Internal Text" }

    { 1100525049;4;DataItem;EstimateLineLoop ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1)) }

    { 1100409003;5;Column;Quantity_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLineQuantity }

    { 1100525041;5;Column;Hours_EstimateLine ;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLineHours }

    { 1100528602;5;Column;CumHours_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CumEstimateLineHours }

    { 1100525023;5;Column;LaborAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLineLaborAmount }

    { 1100528603;5;Column;CumLaborAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CumEstimateLineLaborAmount }

    { 1100525021;5;Column;MaterialAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLineMaterialAmount }

    { 1100528604;5;Column;CumMaterialAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CumEstimateLineMaterialAmount }

    { 1100525022;5;Column;SubcontractingAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount }

    { 1100528605;5;Column;CumSubcontractingAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CumEstimateLineSubcontractingAmount }

    { 1100525020;5;Column;PlantAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLinePlantAmount }

    { 1100528606;5;Column;CumPlantAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CumEstimateLinePlantAmount }

    { 1100525044;5;Column;SundryAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLineSundryAmount }

    { 1100528607;5;Column;CumSundryAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CumEstimateLineSundryAmount }

    { 1100525019;5;Column;Amount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLineAmount }

    { 1100528608;5;Column;CumAmount_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CumEstimateLineAmount }

    { 1100525018;5;Column;CumulativeTotal_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLineCumulativeTotal }

    { 1100528610;5;Column;EstimateLinePartTotal_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=EstimateLinePartTotal }

    { 1100525024;5;Column;Assumption_EstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=Assumption }

    { 1100525085;4;DataItem;CommentLineEstimateLine;
               DataItemTable=Table11020595;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Table Name,Group,No.,Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Estimate Line No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Table Name=CONST(Estimate));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT PrintText THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group),
                            Part=FIELD(Part),
                            Estimate Line No.=FIELD(Line No.) }

    { 1100525084;5;Column;LineNo_CommentLineEstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CommentLineEstimateLine."Line No." }

    { 1100525083;5;Column;Comment_CommentLineEstimateLine;
               SourceExpr=CommentLineEstimateLine.Comment }

    { 1100525008;4;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072075;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Estimate Line,Recipe Group,Recipe,Line No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT PrintRecipeLines THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost) AND
                                     (Quantity = 0) AND
                                     NOT PrintZeroRecipeLines
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales) AND
                                     ("Quantity (Sales)" = 0) AND
                                     NOT PrintZeroRecipeLines
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  DetermineSurchRcpLine("Estimate Recipe Line");

                                  IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
                                    RecipeLineQuantity := Quantity;
                                    RecipeLineHours := Hours;
                                    RecipeLineLaborAmount := "Labor Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLineMaterialAmount := "Material Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLineSubcontractingAmount := "Subcontracting Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLinePlantAmount := "Plant Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLineSundryAmount := "Sundry Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLineAmount := "Cost Amount";
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    RecipeLineQuantity := "Quantity (Sales)";
                                    RecipeLineHours := "Hours (Sales)";
                                    RecipeLineLaborAmount := "Labor Sales Amount";

                                    RecipeLinePlantAmount := "Plant Sales Amount";
                                    RecipeLineSundryAmount := "Sundry Sales Amount";
                                    RecipeLineAmount := "Sales Amount";
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group),

                            Estimate Line=FIELD(Line No.) }

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF "Estimate Line".GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', "Estimate Line".TABLECAPTION, "Estimate Line".GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineSummarySheet@1100485010(Estimate@1100485001 : Record 11012151;VAR SummerySheet@1100525000 : Record 11012172);
    VAR
      NumSheet@1100525001 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      //first determine the concerning Summary Sheet
      IF IgnoreSummary THEN BEGIN
        CLEAR(SummarySheet);
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF SummaryFilter = '' THEN BEGIN
        //db.sn, 03-07-15: C022055
        SummerySheet.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
        SummerySheet.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", '%1', '');
        IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN
          SummarySheet.SETRANGE("Summary Type", SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost)
        ELSE
          SummarySheet.SETRANGE("Summary Type", SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Sales);
        NumSheet := SummerySheet.COUNT;
        IF NumSheet <> 1 THEN
          ERROR(Text999);
        SummerySheet.FINDFIRST;
        //db.en, 03-07-15: C022055
      END ELSE BEGIN
        SummerySheet.GET(Estimate."No.", SummaryFilter);
      END;

      IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN
        SummarySheet.TESTFIELD("Summary Type", SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost)
      ELSE
        SummarySheet.TESTFIELD("Summary Type", SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Sales);

      SummarySheet.CheckAndRefreshSheet;  //db, 17-03-15: C022155
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineSurchEstLine@1100485000(VAR EstimateLine@1100485000 : Record 11072072);
    VAR
      HoursCostOld@1100485002 : Decimal;
      HoursSalesOld@1100525001 : Decimal;
      LaborCostAmountOld@1100485006 : Decimal;
      LaborSalesAmountOld@1100525000 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      //save old values
      HoursCostOld := EstimateLine.Hours;
      HoursSalesOld := EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)";
      LaborCostAmountOld := EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount";
      LaborSalesAmountOld := EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount";

      //determine surcharges for each 'Cost Type' line.
      TempSummarySheetLine1.SETRANGE(Type, TempSummarySheetLine1.Type::"Cost Type");
      IF TempSummarySheetLine1.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          //these are the lines in which the Estimate Line exist
          IF EstLineInSummarySheetLineFilters(EstimateLine, TempSummarySheetLine1) THEN BEGIN
            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Labor) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount", EstimateLine.Hours);
                EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
                EstimateLine.Hours += TotSurchargeHours;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount", EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
                EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" += TotSurchargeHours;
              END;
            END;

            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Material) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount", EstimateLine.Hours);
                EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Material Sales Amount", EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateLine."Material Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END;
            END;

            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Subcontracting) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount", EstimateLine.Hours);
                EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount", EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END;
            END;

            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Plant) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Plant Cost Amount", EstimateLine.Hours);
                EstimateLine."Plant Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Plant Sales Amount", EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateLine."Plant Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END;
            END;

            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Sundry) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Sundry Cost Amount", EstimateLine.Hours);
                EstimateLine."Sundry Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateLine."Sundry Sales Amount", EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateLine."Sundry Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END;
            END;
          END;
        UNTIL TempSummarySheetLine1.NEXT = 0;

      EstimateLine."Cost Amount" :=
        EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" +
        EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount" +
        EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" +
        EstimateLine."Plant Cost Amount" +
        EstimateLine."Sundry Cost Amount";

      EstimateLine."Sales Amount" :=
        EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" +
        EstimateLine."Material Sales Amount" +
        EstimateLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" +
        EstimateLine."Plant Sales Amount" +
        EstimateLine."Sundry Sales Amount";

      IF HoursCostOld <> EstimateLine.Hours THEN
        IF EstimateLine.Quantity <> 0 THEN
          EstimateLine.Norm := EstimateLine.Hours / EstimateLine.Quantity;
      IF HoursSalesOld <> EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" THEN
        IF EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)" <> 0 THEN
          EstimateLine."Norm (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" / EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";

      IF LaborCostAmountOld <> EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" THEN
        IF EstimateLine.Hours <> 0 THEN
          EstimateLine."Cost Rate" := EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" / EstimateLine.Hours;
      IF LaborSalesAmountOld <> EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" THEN
        IF EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" <> 0 THEN
          EstimateLine."Sales Rate" := EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" / EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)";

      IF NOT EstimateLineTotal.GET(
        EstimateLine."Estimate No.", EstimateLine."Sub-Estimate No.",
        EstimateLine."Part Group", EstimateLine.Part, EstimateLine."Line No.") THEN
        EstimateLineTotal.INIT;  //db, 16-01-15: C019505

      IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Hours" := EstimateLine.Hours * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor" := EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material" := EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontracting" := EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant" := EstimateLine."Plant Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry" := EstimateLine."Sundry Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total" := EstimateLine."Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Hours (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Material Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontr. (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Plant Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Sundry Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE EstLineInSummarySheetLineFilters@1100485002(EstimateLine@1100485000 : Record 11072072;SummarySheetLine@1100485001 : Record 11012171) : Boolean;
    VAR
      TempEstimateLine@1100485003 : TEMPORARY Record 11072072;
    BEGIN
      //Determine if Estimate Line fits in filter of the 'Cost Type' line.
      TempEstimateLine := EstimateLine;
      TempEstimateLine.INSERT;

      TempEstimateLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", SummarySheetLine."Estimate No.");
      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", SummarySheetLine."Sub-Estimate Filter");
      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER(Part, SummarySheetLine."Part Filter");
      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status", SummarySheetLine."Line Status Filter");
      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Rate Code", SummarySheetLine."Rate Filter");
      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER(Discipline, SummarySheetLine."Discipline Filter");
      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Trade Speciality", SummarySheetLine."Trade Speciality Filter");
      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Wage Component", SummarySheetLine."Wage Component Filter");
      IF SummarySheetLine."Material Price Filter" <> '' THEN BEGIN
        TempEstimateLine.SETRANGE("Cost Type (Price)", TempEstimateLine."Cost Type (Price)"::Material);
        TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Nett Cost Price", SummarySheetLine."Material Price Filter");
      END;
      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER(Code, SummarySheetLine."Code Filter");

      IF SummarySheetLine."Cost Type" IN
        [SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Labor, SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::"Just Hours", SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Total]
      THEN
        TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Cost Object Labor", SummarySheetLine."Cost Object Filter");

      IF SummarySheetLine."Cost Type" IN
        [SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Material, SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Subcontracting, SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Plant,
         SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Sundry, SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Total]
      THEN
        TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Cost Object Price", SummarySheetLine."Cost Object Filter");

      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER(Recipe, '%1', '');

      EXIT(TempEstimateLine.FINDFIRST);
    END;

    PROCEDURE SummaryLineInFilter@1100485001(SummarySheetLine@1100485000 : Record 11012171;Level@1100485003 : Integer;BaseAmount@1100485004 : Decimal;BaseHours@1100485006 : Decimal);
    VAR
      TempSummarySheetLine@1100485001 : TEMPORARY Record 11012171;
      SummarySheetLine2@1100485002 : Record 11012171;
      SurchargeAmount@1100485005 : Decimal;
      SurchargeHours@1100485007 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      //calculates 1 level subcharge: called recursive!

      TempSummarySheetLine."Estimate No." := SummarySheetLine."Estimate No.";
      TempSummarySheetLine.Summary := SummarySheetLine.Summary;
      TempSummarySheetLine."Row No." := SummarySheetLine."Row No.";
      TempSummarySheetLine.INSERT;

      TempSummarySheetLine2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", SummarySheetLine."Estimate No.");
      TempSummarySheetLine2.SETRANGE(Summary, SummarySheetLine.Summary);
      IF TempSummarySheetLine2.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF TempSummarySheetLine2."Row No." <> SummarySheetLine."Row No." THEN BEGIN
            TempSummarySheetLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", TempSummarySheetLine2."Estimate No.");
            TempSummarySheetLine.SETRANGE(Summary, TempSummarySheetLine2.Summary);
            TempSummarySheetLine.SETFILTER("Row No.", TempSummarySheetLine2."Surcharge Over Row");
            IF TempSummarySheetLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              IF TempSummarySheetLine2.Type = TempSummarySheetLine2.Type::"Surcharge Amount" THEN BEGIN
                SurchargeAmount := BaseAmount * TempSummarySheetLine2."Surcharge Percentage" / 100;
                TotSurchargeAmount += SurchargeAmount;
                SummarySheetLine2.COPY(TempSummarySheetLine2); //Save
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine2, Level + 1, SurchargeAmount, 0);
                TempSummarySheetLine2.COPY(SummarySheetLine2); //Retrieve
              END;
              IF TempSummarySheetLine2.Type = TempSummarySheetLine2.Type::"Surcharge Hours" THEN BEGIN
                SurchargeHours := BaseHours * TempSummarySheetLine2."Surcharge Percentage" / 100;
                IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                  TempSummarySheetLine2.CALCFIELDS("Cost Rate");
                  SurchargeAmount := SurchargeHours * TempSummarySheetLine2."Cost Rate";
                END ELSE BEGIN
                  TempSummarySheetLine2.CALCFIELDS("Sales Rate");
                  SurchargeAmount := SurchargeHours * TempSummarySheetLine2."Sales Rate";
                END;
                TotSurchargeHours += SurchargeHours;
                TotSurchargeAmount += SurchargeAmount;
                SummarySheetLine2.COPY(TempSummarySheetLine2); //Save
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine2, Level + 1, SurchargeAmount, SurchargeHours);
                TempSummarySheetLine2.COPY(SummarySheetLine2); //Retrieve
              END;
            END;
          END;
        UNTIL TempSummarySheetLine2.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineSurchRcpLine@1100485007(VAR EstimateRecipeLine@1100485000 : Record 11072075);
    VAR
      HoursCostOld@1100485006 : Decimal;
      HoursSalesOld@1100525000 : Decimal;
      LaborCostAmountOld@1100485002 : Decimal;
      LaborSalesAmountOld@1100525001 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      //Search concerning Summary Sheet lines

      //save old values
      HoursCostOld := EstimateRecipeLine.Hours;
      HoursSalesOld := EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)";
      LaborCostAmountOld := EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount";
      LaborSalesAmountOld := EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Sales Amount";

      IF EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)" = EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)"::Material THEN BEGIN
        EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Sales Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Sales Amount" := 0;
      END;
      IF EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)" = EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)"::Subcontracting THEN BEGIN
        EstimateRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Sales Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Sales Amount" := 0;
      END;
      IF EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)" = EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)"::Plant THEN BEGIN
        EstimateRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Sales Amount" := 0;
      END;
      IF EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)" = EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)"::Sundry THEN BEGIN
        EstimateRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" := 0;
        EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Sales Amount" := 0;
      END;

      //Determine subcharges for each "Cost Type" line.
      TempSummarySheetLine1.SETRANGE(Type, TempSummarySheetLine1.Type::"Cost Type");
      IF TempSummarySheetLine1.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          //these are the lines in which the Estimate Line exist.
          IF RcptLineInSummarySheetLineFilters(EstimateRecipeLine, TempSummarySheetLine1) THEN BEGIN
            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Labor) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount", EstimateRecipeLine.Hours);
                EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
                EstimateRecipeLine.Hours += TotSurchargeHours;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Sales Amount", EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
                EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)" += TotSurchargeHours;
              END;
            END;
            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Material) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount", EstimateRecipeLine.Hours);
                EstimateRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount", EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END;
            END;
            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Subcontracting) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount", EstimateRecipeLine.Hours);
                EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount", EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END;
            END;
            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Plant) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount", EstimateRecipeLine.Hours);
                EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Sales Amount", EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END;
            END;
            IF (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Sundry) OR
               (TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type" = TempSummarySheetLine1."Cost Type"::Total)
            THEN BEGIN
              TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
              TotSurchargeHours := 0;
              IF SummarySheet."Summary Type" = SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost THEN BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Cost Amount", EstimateRecipeLine.Hours);
                EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Cost Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                SummaryLineInFilter(TempSummarySheetLine1, 0, EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Sales Amount", EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)");
                EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Sales Amount" += TotSurchargeAmount;
              END;
            END;
          END;
        UNTIL TempSummarySheetLine1.NEXT = 0;

      EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Amount" :=
        EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" +
        EstimateRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" +
        EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" +
        EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" +
        EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Cost Amount";

      EstimateRecipeLine."Sales Amount" :=
        EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Sales Amount" +
        EstimateRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount" +
        EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" +
        EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Sales Amount" +
        EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Sales Amount";

      IF HoursCostOld <> EstimateRecipeLine.Hours THEN
        IF EstimateRecipeLine.Quantity <> 0 THEN
          EstimateRecipeLine.Norm := EstimateRecipeLine.Hours / EstimateRecipeLine.Quantity;
      IF HoursSalesOld <> EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)" THEN
        IF EstimateRecipeLine."Quantity (Sales)" <> 0 THEN
          EstimateRecipeLine."Norm (Sales)" := EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)"/ EstimateRecipeLine."Quantity (Sales)";

      IF LaborCostAmountOld <> EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" THEN
        IF EstimateRecipeLine.Hours <> 0 THEN
          EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Rate" := EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" / EstimateRecipeLine.Hours;
      IF LaborSalesAmountOld <> EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Sales Amount" THEN
        IF EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)" <> 0 THEN
          EstimateRecipeLine."Sales Rate" := EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Sales Amount" / EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)";
    END;

    PROCEDURE RcptLineInSummarySheetLineFilters@1100485008(EstimateRecipeLine@1100485000 : Record 11072075;SummarySheetLine@1100485001 : Record 11012171) : Boolean;
    VAR
      TempEstimateRecipeLine@1100485003 : TEMPORARY Record 11072075;
    BEGIN
      //Determine if Estimate Line fits in filter of the 'Cost Type' line.
      TempEstimateRecipeLine := EstimateRecipeLine;
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.INSERT;

      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", SummarySheetLine."Estimate No.");
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", SummarySheetLine."Sub-Estimate Filter");
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER(Part, SummarySheetLine."Part Filter");
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER("Line Status", SummarySheetLine."Line Status Filter");
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER("Rate Code", SummarySheetLine."Rate Filter");
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER(Discipline, SummarySheetLine."Discipline Filter");
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER("Trade Speciality", SummarySheetLine."Trade Speciality Filter");
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER("Wage Component", SummarySheetLine."Wage Component Filter");
      IF SummarySheetLine."Material Price Filter" <> '' THEN BEGIN
        TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Cost Type (Price)", TempEstimateRecipeLine."Cost Type (Price)"::Material);
        TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER("Nett Cost Price", SummarySheetLine."Material Price Filter");
      END;
      TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER(Code, SummarySheetLine."Code Filter");

      IF SummarySheetLine."Cost Type" IN
        [SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Labor, SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::"Just Hours", SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Total]
      THEN
        TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER("Cost Object Labor", SummarySheetLine."Cost Object Filter");

      IF SummarySheetLine."Cost Type" IN
        [SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Material, SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Subcontracting, SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Plant,
         SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Sundry, SummarySheetLine."Cost Type"::Total]
      THEN
        TempEstimateRecipeLine.SETFILTER("Cost Object Price", SummarySheetLine."Cost Object Filter");

      EXIT(TempEstimateRecipeLine.FINDFIRST);
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineAmountRecipeEstLine@1100485017(VAR EstimateLine@1100485000 : Record 11072072);
    VAR
      EstimateRecipeLine@1100525000 : Record 11072075;
    BEGIN
      EstimateLine.Hours := 0;
      EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Plant Cost Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Sundry Cost Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Cost Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine.Norm := 0;
      EstimateLine."Cost Rate" := 0;

      EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Material Sales Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Plant Sales Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Sundry Sales Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Sales Amount" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Norm (Sales)" := 0;
      EstimateLine."Sales Rate" := 0;

      EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", EstimateLine."Estimate No.");
      EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", EstimateLine."Sub-Estimate No.");
      EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Part Group", EstimateLine."Part Group");
      EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE(Part, EstimateLine.Part);
      EstimateRecipeLine.SETRANGE("Estimate Line", EstimateLine."Line No.");
      IF EstimateRecipeLine.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          DetermineSurchRcpLine(EstimateRecipeLine);

          EstimateLine.Hours += EstimateRecipeLine.Hours * EstimateLine.Quantity;
          EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Cost Amount" * EstimateLine.Quantity;
          EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Material Cost Amount" * EstimateLine.Quantity;
          EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * EstimateLine.Quantity;
          EstimateLine."Plant Cost Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Cost Amount" * EstimateLine.Quantity;
          EstimateLine."Sundry Cost Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Cost Amount" * EstimateLine.Quantity;
          EstimateLine."Cost Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Cost Amount" * EstimateLine.Quantity;

          EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" += EstimateRecipeLine."Hours (Sales)" * EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";
          EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Labor Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";
          EstimateLine."Material Sales Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Material Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";
          EstimateLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";
          EstimateLine."Plant Sales Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Plant Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";
          EstimateLine."Sundry Sales Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Sundry Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";
          EstimateLine."Sales Amount" += EstimateRecipeLine."Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";
        UNTIL EstimateRecipeLine.NEXT = 0;

      IF EstimateLine.Quantity <> 0 THEN
        EstimateLine.Norm := EstimateLine.Hours / EstimateLine.Quantity;
      IF EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)" <> 0 THEN
        EstimateLine."Norm (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" / EstimateLine."Quantity (Sales)";

      IF EstimateLine.Hours <> 0 THEN
        EstimateLine."Cost Rate" := EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" / EstimateLine.Hours;
      IF EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" <> 0 THEN
        EstimateLine."Sales Rate" := EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" / EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)";

      IF NOT EstimateLineTotal.GET(
        EstimateLine."Estimate No.", EstimateLine."Sub-Estimate No.",
        EstimateLine."Part Group", EstimateLine.Part, EstimateLine."Line No.") THEN
        EstimateLineTotal.INIT;  //db, 16-01-15: C019505

      IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Hours" := EstimateLine.Hours * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor" := EstimateLine."Labor Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material" := EstimateLine."Material Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontracting" := EstimateLine."Subcontracting Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant" := EstimateLine."Plant Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry" := EstimateLine."Sundry Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total" := EstimateLine."Cost Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Hours (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Hours (Sales)" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Labor (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Labor Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Material (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Material Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Subcontr. (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Subcontracting Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Plant (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Plant Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Sundry (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Sundry Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
        EstimateLineTotal."Cumulative Total (Sales)" := EstimateLine."Sales Amount" * EstimateLine."Part Quantity";
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE EstLineInLineStatusFilter@1100525001(EstimateLine@1100525000 : Record 11072072) : Boolean;
    VAR
      TempEstimateLine@1100525001 : TEMPORARY Record 11072072;
    BEGIN
      TempEstimateLine := EstimateLine;
      TempEstimateLine.INSERT;

      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status", LineStatusFilter);

      EXIT(TempEstimateLine.FINDFIRST);
    END;

    PROCEDURE EnableFields@1100525002();
    BEGIN
      PrintRecipeLinesEnabled := PrintEstimateLines;
      PrintZeroLinesEnabled := PrintEstimateLines;
      PrintZeroRecipeLinesEnabled := PrintRecipeLines;
      TotalsPerChapterEnabled := NOT PrintRecipeLines;
      SummaryFilterEnabled := NOT IgnoreSummary;
      PrintAssumptionSeparatelyEnabled := NOT PrintEstimateLines;
      LineStatusFilterEnabled := PrintAssumptionSeparately;
      PrintSurchargeInformationEnabled := NOT IgnoreSummary;
    END;

    PROCEDURE LookupSummaryFilter@1100525007();
    VAR
      SummarySheetRec2@1100525000 : Record 11012172;
    BEGIN
      //db, 19-05-11: C015230
      IF "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No.") <> '' THEN
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
      SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Summary Type", PrintTotalsBasedOn);
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Summary Sheet List",SummarySheetRec2) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
        SummaryFilter := SummarySheetRec2.Summary;
        ValidateSummaryFilter;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ValidateSummaryFilter@1100525006();
    VAR
      SummarySheetRec2@1100525000 : Record 11012172;
    BEGIN
      //db, 19-05-11: C015230
      IF "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No.") <> '' THEN BEGIN
        //filter on main table only set if report called from estimate; manual change will be evaluated later
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE(Summary, SummaryFilter);
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Summary Type", PrintTotalsBasedOn);
        SummarySheetRec2.FINDSET;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckRelationSummaryEstimate@1100525005();
    VAR
      SummarySheetRec2@1100525000 : Record 11012172;
    BEGIN
      //db, 08-05-11: C015230
      IF IgnoreSummary THEN BEGIN
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF SummaryFilter <>'' THEN BEGIN
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE(Summary,SummaryFilter);
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
        IF NOT SummarySheetRec2.FINDFIRST THEN
          ERROR(Text002);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
        IF NOT SummarySheetRec2.FINDFIRST THEN
          IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Summary Sheet List",SummarySheetRec2) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
            SummaryFilter := SummarySheetRec2.Summary;
      END;

      IF SummarySheetRec2."Sub-Estimate No." <> "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.") THEN BEGIN
        IF CheckFilterSubEstimate(SummarySheetRec2, "Estimate Line") = FALSE THEN //db, 20-10-09: M16782
          ERROR(Text001);  //db, 08-06-09: M15541
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckFilterSubEstimate@1100525004(VAR SumRec@1100525002 : Record 11012172;VAR EstLineRec@1100525003 : Record 11072072) : Boolean;
    VAR
      SubEstRec@1100525000 : Record 11072074;
      TmpSubEstRec@1100525001 : TEMPORARY Record 11072074;
      SumLineRec@1100525004 : Record 11012171;
      LastFilter@1100525005 : Text[1000];
    BEGIN
      //db, 20-10-09: M16782
      SumLineRec.SETFILTER("Estimate No.", SumRec."Estimate No.");
      SumLineRec.SETFILTER(Summary, SumRec.Summary);
      SumLineRec.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate Filter", '<>%1', '');
      IF SumLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF LastFilter <> SumLineRec."Sub-Estimate Filter" THEN BEGIN
            SubEstRec.SETFILTER("Estimate No.", SumLineRec."Estimate No.");
            SubEstRec.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", SumLineRec."Sub-Estimate Filter");
            IF SubEstRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
              REPEAT
                TmpSubEstRec.COPY(SubEstRec);
                IF TmpSubEstRec.INSERT THEN;
              UNTIL SubEstRec.NEXT = 0;
            END;
          END;
          LastFilter := SumLineRec."Sub-Estimate Filter";
        UNTIL SumLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      SubEstRec.SETFILTER("Estimate No.", EstLineRec.GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
      SubEstRec.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", EstLineRec.GETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No."));
      IF SubEstRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF NOT TmpSubEstRec.GET(SubEstRec."Estimate No.", SubEstRec."Sub-Estimate No.") THEN EXIT(FALSE);
          TmpSubEstRec.DELETE;
        UNTIL SubEstRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      IF TmpSubEstRec.COUNT <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE)
      ELSE
        EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      Page break per group is not activated for Group of tablix1. For some strange reason printing does not go right when there are more
      estimate lines then fits on one page. As only 1 estimate will be printed each time, this should not be a problem.
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
